        <h1>Major prize to tuberculosis researcher</h1>

<p><img alt="Maria Lerm" class="img_right"   src="http://www.liu.se/ny-mall-2012/liu-s-startnyheter/1.588016/maria-lermpuff.jpg" />Maria Lerm, associate professor in medical microbiology, has been awarded the Swedish Fernstr&#246;m Prize of SEK 100,000. She wins the prize for her research aimed at developing a better vaccine for tuberculosis &#8211; a disease that kills two million people every year.</p>

<p><a  href="http://www.liu.se/liu-nytt/arkiv/nyhetsarkiv/1.587595?l=en">Article in full</a></p>


<h1 class="list-item news">The fading of compassion</h1>

<p class="list-item news"><img alt="Undern√§rt barn matas" class="img_right"   src="http://www.liu.se/ny-mall-2012/liu-s-startnyheter/1.586095/undernartbarn.220.jpg" />The more people who beg for our compassion, the colder we become. The desire to give is strongest towards one person, or to a single identifiable unit.&#160;The physiological mechanisms behind this behaviour have now been documented by Daniel V&#228;stfj&#228;ll, professor of psychology at LiU, together with fellow researchers in the United States. (Picture from Wikipedia.)</p>

<p><a  href="http://www.liu.se/forskning/forskningsnyheter/1.585536?l=en">Article in full</a></p>

<h2 class="vinjett">EVENTS</h2>

<h3><a href="http://www.internetaudiology.eu/">Internet &amp; audiology</a></h3>

<p><strong>3-4 Oct</strong></p>

<p>The First International Meeting on Internet and Audiology. Researchers and others with an interest for the broad topic of internet and audiology are invited. No conference fee.</p>

<p>Location: Link&#246;ping University, Campus Valla</p>

<p>For more info contact:<br />
<a href="mailto:gerhard.andersson@liu.se?subject=International%20meeting%20on%20internet%20%26%20audiology">Gerhard Andersson</a></p>

<p><strong>15-17 October</strong></p>

<p>CEDER&#160;&#8211; Center for dementia research - organises the international conference &quot;Life with dementia: relations&quot;</p>

<p>Location: Norrk&#246;ping</p>

<p>For more info contact:<br />
